The objective is simple yet compelling: slide tiles on a 4x4 grid to merge matching numbers, doubling their values with each combination, until you reach the coveted 2048 tile.\r\n\r\nThis browser-based puzzle game has captivated millions of players worldwide with its elegant mechanics and endless replayability. Starting with two tiles displaying the number 2, players swipe in four directions (up, down, left, right) to move all tiles simultaneously. When two tiles with the same number collide, they merge into one tile with their combined value (2+2=4, 4+4=8, 8+8=16, and so on).\r\n\r\nThe game continues beyond 2048, allowing skilled players to pursue even higher scores by creating 4096, 8192, or larger tiles. Strategic thinking and careful planning are essential, as every move spawns a new tile (either 2 or 4) in a random empty space. The game ends when the grid fills completely with no possible moves remaining.\r\n\r\nPerfect for quick mental exercises or extended puzzle-solving sessions, 2048 offers smooth gameplay on both desktop and mobile devices. No downloads or installations required - simply play directly in your browser. Whether you're a casual gamer looking for a brief distraction or a puzzle enthusiast seeking to master the perfect strategy, 2048 provides endless entertainment and mental stimulation.\r\n\r\nAs an open-source project, 2048 is freely available to the community.
